<Rate>3<//Rate><name>Debbie Flores< /name><Time>1488587861938< /Time><Text>I went to Dr Garry Regier's office today for my annual eye examination. This is the second time I've gone to Dr. Reiger's office as I was pretty pleased with my first visit. However, this time around, Dr. Regier suggested I try contacts during my annual examination. Please keep in mind I had no intention, nor had I considered contacts prior to his suggestion. He gave me his professional opinion and thoroughly explained the benefits of what might be if I tried contacts. I was hesitant at first but decided to give contacts a try based on his experienced opinion. However, Dr. Regier never mentioned it would be a separate fee to go through the contact consultation. So, when I was checking out, I was surprised at how much my bill was. I respectfully voiced my concern to the receptionist and to Dr. Regier after paying my bill. I said I was a little upset that no one told me there would be an extra fee for the contact consultation. I understand miscommunication can happen, however I was VERY DISTURBED by Dr. Regier's response - "Nothing is free." Voicing my concern does not equate to wanting a free service, nor was I suggesting the consultation should have been free. I voiced my concern because I don't think a service should be suggested without being transparent about associated costs.  As a consumer, I think it's fair to expect transparency from any service provider.</Text>< userid>

<Rate>1<//Rate><Review>So when I locked myself out recently, tis service turned up on a smartphone google search and I called them.  Accented guy answers the phone and says it'll be $15 for the service call, and then $35 or up depending on the kind of lock.  He'll be here in 15 minutes.

<Rate>5< /Rate><Text>Great experience! The staff was incredibly friendly and helpful, they gave a great tour of the menu including specials and substitutions for vegetarians in our party.

The food itself was excellent; they say the mole is cooked for three days and it shows! Incredible depth of flavor, the kind of place you want to scrape every drop of sauce with leftover chips.

I usually don‚Äôt prefer corn tortillas even though it‚Äôs more traditional, but the fresh, hand-made ones here are absolutely to die for.

Finally their drink menu was really varied and interesting. Seems like everything they offer pairs well. I got the Santa Iguana, which was very refreshing and vegetal, and complemented the rich and earthy mole.

The only difficulty is of course seating. There are currently Covid restrictions, so not a fault of the restaurant. To their credit, they have a lovely outdoor patio with great atmosphere and music. I made a reservation in the morning day-of, but I saw people turned away at the door who tried to walk up and get seated on a weekend night. Just make a reservation and you should be fine!

Overall, highly recommend!<//Text>< Pictures>

<Name>Wilson</Name><date>1610698594091<//date><rating>5<//rating><review>You wrote a review for Kansai Ramen & Sushi House
38 minutes ago
5.0 star rating
1/14/2021

PEOPLE, PEOPLE, people, let me tell you about Kansai Ramen & Sushi. The Ramen is worth the visit alone. I do not know about the sushi, because when I first went ordered from this place, I was looking for some good ramen to eat. And let me tell you, I was not disappointed. I have had worse ramen in Tokyo than in Kansai. This place is a legit Ramen shop. I have always been meaning to try the sushi, but every time I walk in the ramen calls my name like a siren calling me from the sea of flavors. Though I have not tried the sushi, I can tell you if it is half as good as the ramen, should receive 6 stars. I cannot express to you the joy I had upon discovering this restaurant. It is a Stellar place, with AMAZING ramen and great service. I would have pictures of the food, but every time I order from there, I instantly dig in. Not to mention they have some great Karage, most places have a poor imitation of it. But not here, this place is great, a go to recommend. You  are doing yourself a disservice if you are trying to find some ramen and NOT visit. <Rating>5</Rating>< text>
Service: Excellent! Went with large party, called ahead and they were willing to save us a table which was awesome since I called another ramen place in Sacramento and they refused.
Food: Delicious! I had the Pork belly ramen; noodles could be a lil more el dante but still good nonetheless, broth was tasty and the 3 pieces of  pork belly we're nicely charred on the outside and we'll seasoned. The rest of my party had Karaage ramen, Miso Ramen, Seafood ramen, their special item: Brisket ramen, tempura don, unagi don, handrolls, everyone enjoyed their food.
Price: The special item was $15. The other bowls of ramen were $10.95 each which are very reasonable since most ramen places in SF and the cities around the bay area charge on average $14/bowl.
Overall a great and satisfying experience, will definitely be back!</text>

<pictures>None< /pictures><response>None</response><rating>5<//rating><UserId.>113822788770219085107< /UserId.><time>1516687368318< /time><GmapID>0x809adabe0f576211:0x7ffe4ad092b2b8c4</GmapID>< Review>
When I visited Kansai, my partner and I shared the seafood ramen, agedashi tofu, and the chef's special basil salmon sashimi. The ramen was pretty par for the course, but definitely satisfying,  the tofu was good, though it would be nice if it was cut into more manageable chunks. The sashimi was the reason I give this 5 stars, it was absolutely delicious! The sauce wasn't overpowering so we could taste the flavor and freshness of the fish. Also, the wait staff was very relaxed and pleasant, and our food came out quickly in spite of the restaurant being nearly full to capacity. I definitely plan on returning.< /Review>

< Text>
Came here for lunch between wine tasting and was pleasantly surprised.  Our server was this funny older blonde woman who was very attentive and very good.  She was a welcome change from what we have had at other Chili's.  We ordered the Buffalo Cauliflower to start and were surprised at how much we enjoyed it, so much so we made the mistake of ordering it again.  Not that the 2nd batch was worse, just too much food.  A great vegetarian appetizer for sure, I would like to see them maybe do a healthier grilled version if possible, but it was damn good nonetheless.  As for my main meal I ordered the Buffalo Chicken Ranch Sandwich since I wanted something hearty but not as heavy as a burger.  The sandwich was okay, nothing special though.  As you can see in the picture the chicken looked over cooked and the sandwich overall just didn't look appealing.  Tasted decent enough, but I don't think I'd order it again.  Overall a good experience though, clean restaurant and the server we had really helped make this a good trip.< /Text>

< text>
The food is ok but is no different than any other large restaurant chain. Their menu is almost predictable and their waitstaff is at least consistent. Consistently poor in the quality of service provided by 90% of them. No training is done, and if it is, its a complete failure of a program. Waiters will forget things requested or bring the wrong item.

I am not a fan of how your food is brought out by someone other than your waiter. This system of servicing customers is flawed in my ways, but I will speak of only one. Because the individual serving your orders didn't take the order, they can't possibly know anything that you communicated to your waiter when they were taking your order. So any special instructions will probably get lost in the shuffle.

Bottom line is the food is consistently average and never surprisingly great. < Review>
First, let me say that the servers and the food have always been great. The problem with Chili's is that the ordering system and table kiosk payment system has got to go! DO NOT go there with more than two people or where you will need to split the check. First, the ordering system is stupid. We frequently go with groups of 8-10. The poor server, using a system corporate forced upon them, has to go around the entire table getting appetizers, then go around again and get entrees, etc., etc. When you are trying to split the ticket, this makes it impossible to keep it straight. We have NEVER had it come out correctly using the system. What happened to going around the table and getting each individuals ENTIRE order? Second, the kiosk...brilliant concept, horrible execution. It NEVER works correctly. When you try to split the ticket manually(easy enough) and then pay, it is all messed up and not split the way you did it! I complained to corporate HQ about this, telling them the system they are forcing the individual restaurants to use was messed up and, predictably, I get a response email saying they have forwarded my comments to the restaurant. Idiots. Bottom line, if you go with more than two people, allow just as much time to order and pay as you do for the actual meal.< /Review>

<Rate>1< /Rate>< Text>
My wife, 2 year old son and I were up visiting family and we arrived in town a little early, so we decided to grab a bite to eat.  What better place than Chili's, right?  That's what we thought, but were proven wrong.

When we walked in, we thought it was going to be quick because the place was pretty empty.  We got seated and it took our server almost 10 minutes to come over just to get a ‚Äúhello.‚Äù  Another 10 minutes and we finally got our drinks and placed our order.  Usually 10 minutes isn't that long, but when you have a cranky 2 year old who was cooped up in a car for a 4 hour ride, it feels like an eternity.  Especially when he's also a little hungry.

When our order came, the server forgot to put in his simple quesadilla order.  Granted, she was apologetic, but come on.  Really?  Another 15 minutes later my boy was eating his quesadilla.  Yes, 15 minutes for a regular cheese quesadilla....  And the place is virtually empty, still.

When we were done, they apologized again and took the quesadilla off the bill.  That kind of made up for it, but it took them 10 minutes to come and get it to run my card.  After that, guess how long it took to get my receipt......?  Yup, 10 minutes.

To say hat we will never be back to this Chili's is an understatement.<//Text>

< Review>
Valentine's day. Enough said. I work in food service and I can empathize with many reasons why things don't come out ok, but never do you tell a customer as a manager "we are in over our heads" as an excuse for why I had to wait an extra 20 mins for my food because your kitchen didn't "read the ticket correctly". That's a cop out excuse for incompetence. Just be a manager and take accountability for the mistake by TALKING to the customer. Instead we were told this BS and then waited for our order. It was a salad, a chicken wings side, a sandwich (which was forgotten), and a dessert. We arrived home to find the salad wilted, the ice cream in the dessert almost melted completely, and the side that I asked for (on the sandwich that was forgotten) not there.
I called the manager, his name is guy, and I was offered coupons. Where was he when the FIRST mistake was made. A mediocre response to a mediocre experience. At least that's something that's consistent. Never going back. I'm calling corporate and hopefully they will do something to fix this issue.
